<s> soft and even unemphatic good morning sir <\s>
<s> about your husband he's not in work i hear <\s>
<s> no sir of course he's not in work just now <\s>
<s> then i suppose he's earning nothing <\s>
<s> no sir he's not earning anything just now sir <\s>
<s> and how many children have you <\s>
<s> three children but of course they don't eat very much sir <\s>
<s> a little silence barthwick <\s>
<s> and how old is the eldest <\s>
<s> nine years old sir <\s>
<s> do they go to school <\s>
<s> jones yes sir they all three go to school every day <\s>
<s> severely and what about their food when you're out at work <\s>
<s> well sir i have to give them their dinner to take with them <\s>
<s> of course i m not always able to give them anything sometimes i have to send them without but my husband is very good about the children when he's in work <\s>
<s> but when he's not in work of course he's a very difficult man <\s>
<s> he drinks i suppose <\s>
<s> of course i can't say he does n't drink because he does <\s>
<s> and i suppose he takes all your money <\s>
<s> no sir he's very good about my money except when he's not himself and then of course he treats me very badly <\s>
<s> now what is he your husband <\s>
<s> by profession sir of course he's a groom <\s>
<s> how came he to lose his place <\s>
<s> he lost his place a long time ago sir and he's never had a very long job since and now of course the motor cars are against him <\s>
<s> when were you married to him mrs <\s>
<s> eight years ago sir that was in mrs <\s>
<s> you said the eldest child was nine <\s>
<s> yes ma'am of course that was why he lost his place <\s>
<s> he did n't treat me rightly and of course his employer said he couldn't keep him because of the example <\s>
<s> you mean he ahem mrs <\s>
<s> yes sir and of course after he lost his place he married me <\s>
<s> you actually mean to say you you were barthwick <\s>
<s> hurriedly and where are you living now mrs <\s>
<s> we've not got a home sir <\s>
<s> of course we've been obliged to put away most of our things <\s>
<s> put your things away <\s>
<s> you mean to to er to pawn them <\s>
<s> yes sir to put them away <\s>
<s> we're living in merthyr street that is close by here sir at no <\s>
<s> we just have the one room <\s>
<s> and what do you pay a week <\s>
<s> we pay six shillings a week sir for a furnished room <\s>
<s> and i suppose you're behind in the rent <\s>
<s> yes sir we're a little behind in the rent <\s>
<s> but you're in good work aren't you <\s>
<s> well sir i have a day in stamford place thursdays <\s>
<s> and mondays and wednesdays and fridays i come here <\s>
<s> but to day of course is a half day because of yesterday's bank holiday <\s>
<s> i see four days a week and you get half a crown a day is that it <\s>
<s> yes sir and my dinner but sometimes it's only half a day and that's eighteen pence <\s>
<s> and when your husband earns anything he spends it in drink i suppose <\s>
<s> sometimes he does sir and sometimes he gives it to me for the children <\s>
<s> of course he would work if he could get it sir but it seems there are a great many people out of work <\s>
<s> we er won't go into that <\s>
<s> sympathetically and how about your work here <\s>
<s> do you find it hard <\s>
<s> no sir not very hard sir except of course when i don't get my sleep at night <\s>
<s> and you help do all the rooms <\s>
<s> and sometimes i suppose you go out for cook <\s>
<s> and you ve been out this morning <\s>
<s> yes sir of course i had to go to the greengrocer's <\s>
<s> so your husband earns nothing <\s>
<s> and he's a bad character <\s>
<s> no sir i don't say that sir <\s>
<s> i think there's a great deal of good in him though he does treat me very bad sometimes <\s>
<s> and of course i don't like to leave him but i think i ought to because really i hardly know how to stay with him <\s>
<s> he often raises his hand to me <\s>
<s> not long ago he gave me a blow here touches her breast and i can feel it now <\s>
<s> so i think i ought to leave him don't you sir <\s>
<s> i can't help you there <\s>
<s> it's a very serious thing to leave your husband <\s>
<s> yes sir of course i m afraid of what he might do to me if i were to leave him he can be so very violent <\s>
<s> well that i can't pretend to say anything about <\s>
<s> it's the bad principle i'm speaking of mrs <\s>
<s> yes sir i know nobody can help me <\s>
<s> i know i must decide for myself and of course i know that he has a very hard life <\s>
<s> and he's fond of the children and its very hard for him to see them going without food <\s>
<s> hastily well er thank you i just wanted to hear about you <\s>
<s> i don't think i need detain you any longer mrs <\s>
<s> no sir thank you sir <\s>
<s> good morning sir good morning ma'am <\s>
<s> exchanging glances with his wife by the way mrs <\s>
<s> jones i think it is only fair to tell you a silver cigarette box er is missing <\s>
<s> looking from one face to the other i am very sorry sir <\s>
<s> yes you have not seen it i suppose <\s>
<s> realising that suspicion is upon her with an uneasy movement where was it sir if you please sir <\s>
<s> evasively where did marlow say <\s>
<s> er in this room yes in this room <\s>
<s> no sir i have n't seen it of course if i d seen it i should have noticed it <\s>
<s> giving hey a rapid glance you you are sure of that <\s>
<s> with a slow nodding of her head i have not seen it and of course i don't know where it is <\s>
<s> she turns and goes quietly out barthwick <\s>

<s> act ii scene i the jones's lodgings merthyr street at half past two o'clock <\s>
<s> the bare room with tattered oilcloth and damp distempered walls has an air of tidy wretchedness <\s>
<s> on the bed lies jones half dressed his coat is thrown across his feet and muddy boots are lying on the floor close by <\s>
<s> the door is opened and mrs <\s>
<s> jones comes in dressed in a pinched black jacket and old black sailor hat she carries a parcel wrapped up in the times <\s>
<s> she puts her parcel down unwraps an apron half a loaf two onions three potatoes and a tiny piece of bacon <\s>
<s> taking a teapot from the cupboard she rinses it shakes into it some powdered tea out of a screw of paper puts it on the hearth and sitting in a wooden chair quietly begins to cry <\s>
<s> soft and even unemphatic good morning sir <\s>
<s> about your husband he's not in work i hear <\s>
<s> no sir of course he's not in work just now <\s>
<s> then i suppose he's earning nothing <\s>
<s> no sir he's not earning anything just now sir <\s>
<s> and how many children have you <\s>
<s> three children but of course they don't eat very much sir <\s>
<s> a little silence barthwick <\s>
<s> and how old is the eldest <\s>
<s> nine years old sir <\s>
<s> do they go to school <\s>
<s> jones yes sir they all three go to school every day <\s>
<s> severely and what about their food when you're out at work <\s>
<s> well sir i have to give them their dinner to take with them <\s>
<s> of course i m not always able to give them anything sometimes i have to send them without but my husband is very good about the children when he's in work <\s>
<s> but when he's not in work of course he's a very difficult man <\s>
<s> he drinks i suppose <\s>
<s> of course i can't say he does n't drink because he does <\s>
<s> and i suppose he takes all your money <\s>
<s> no sir he's very good about my money except when he's not himself and then of course he treats me very badly <\s>
<s> now what is he your husband <\s>
<s> by profession sir of course he's a groom <\s>
<s> how came he to lose his place <\s>
<s> he lost his place a long time ago sir and he's never had a very long job since and now of course the motor cars are against him <\s>
<s> when were you married to him mrs <\s>
<s> eight years ago sir that was in mrs <\s>
<s> you said the eldest child was nine <\s>
<s> yes ma'am of course that was why he lost his place <\s>
<s> he did n't treat me rightly and of course his employer said he couldn't keep him because of the example <\s>
<s> you mean he ahem mrs <\s>
<s> yes sir and of course after he lost his place he married me <\s>
<s> you actually mean to say you you were barthwick <\s>
<s> hurriedly and where are you living now mrs <\s>
<s> we've not got a home sir <\s>
<s> of course we've been obliged to put away most of our things <\s>
<s> put your things away <\s>
<s> you mean to to er to pawn them <\s>
<s> yes sir to put them away <\s>
<s> we're living in merthyr street that is close by here sir at no <\s>
<s> we just have the one room <\s>
<s> and what do you pay a week <\s>
<s> we pay six shillings a week sir for a furnished room <\s>
<s> and i suppose you're behind in the rent <\s>
<s> yes sir we're a little behind in the rent <\s>
<s> but you're in good work aren't you <\s>
<s> well sir i have a day in stamford place thursdays <\s>
<s> and mondays and wednesdays and fridays i come here <\s>
<s> but to day of course is a half day because of yesterday's bank holiday <\s>
<s> i see four days a week and you get half a crown a day is that it <\s>
<s> yes sir and my dinner but sometimes it's only half a day and that's eighteen pence <\s>
<s> and when your husband earns anything he spends it in drink i suppose <\s>
<s> sometimes he does sir and sometimes he gives it to me for the children <\s>
<s> of course he would work if he could get it sir but it seems there are a great many people out of work <\s>
<s> we er won't go into that <\s>
<s> sympathetically and how about your work here <\s>
<s> do you find it hard <\s>
<s> no sir not very hard sir except of course when i don't get my sleep at night <\s>
<s> and you help do all the rooms <\s>
<s> and sometimes i suppose you go out for cook <\s>
<s> and you ve been out this morning <\s>
<s> yes sir of course i had to go to the greengrocer's <\s>
<s> so your husband earns nothing <\s>
<s> and he's a bad character <\s>
<s> no sir i don't say that sir <\s>
<s> i think there's a great deal of good in him though he does treat me very bad sometimes <\s>
<s> and of course i don't like to leave him but i think i ought to because really i hardly know how to stay with him <\s>
<s> he often raises his hand to me <\s>
<s> not long ago he gave me a blow here touches her breast and i can feel it now <\s>
<s> so i think i ought to leave him don't you sir <\s>
<s> i can't help you there <\s>
<s> it's a very serious thing to leave your husband <\s>
<s> yes sir of course i m afraid of what he might do to me if i were to leave him he can be so very violent <\s>
<s> well that i can't pretend to say anything about <\s>
<s> it's the bad principle i'm speaking of mrs <\s>
<s> yes sir i know nobody can help me <\s>
<s> i know i must decide for myself and of course i know that he has a very hard life <\s>
<s> and he's fond of the children and its very hard for him to see them going without food <\s>
<s> hastily well er thank you i just wanted to hear about you <\s>
<s> i don't think i need detain you any longer mrs <\s>
<s> no sir thank you sir <\s>
<s> good morning sir good morning ma'am <\s>
<s> exchanging glances with his wife by the way mrs <\s>
<s> jones i think it is only fair to tell you a silver cigarette box er is missing <\s>

<s> yes sir of course i had to go to the greengrocer's <\s>
<s> so your husband earns nothing <\s>
<s> and he's a bad character <\s>
<s> no sir i don't say that sir <\s>
<s> i think there's a great deal of good in him though he does treat me very bad sometimes <\s>
<s> and of course i don't like to leave him but i think i ought to because really i hardly know how to stay with him <\s>
<s> he often raises his hand to me <\s>
<s> not long ago he gave me a blow here touches her breast and i can feel it now <\s>
<s> so i think i ought to leave him don't you sir <\s>
<s> i can't help you there <\s>
<s> it's a very serious thing to leave your husband <\s>
<s> yes sir of course i m afraid of what he might do to me if i were to leave him he can be so very violent <\s>
<s> well that i can't pretend to say anything about <\s>
<s> it's the bad principle i'm speaking of mrs <\s>
<s> yes sir i know nobody can help me <\s>
<s> i know i must decide for myself and of course i know that he has a very hard life <\s>
<s> and he's fond of the children and its very hard for him to see them going without food <\s>
<s> hastily well er thank you i just wanted to hear about you <\s>
<s> i don't think i need detain you any longer mrs <\s>
<s> no sir thank you sir <\s>
<s> good morning sir good morning ma'am <\s>
<s> exchanging glances with his wife by the way mrs <\s>
<s> jones i think it is only fair to tell you a silver cigarette box er is missing <\s>
<s> looking from one face to the other i am very sorry sir <\s>
<s> yes you have not seen it i suppose <\s>
<s> realising that suspicion is upon her with an uneasy movement where was it sir if you please sir <\s>
<s> evasively where did marlow say <\s>
<s> er in this room yes in this room <\s>
<s> no sir i have n't seen it of course if i d seen it i should have noticed it <\s>
<s> giving hey a rapid glance you you are sure of that <\s>
<s> with a slow nodding of her head i have not seen it and of course i don't know where it is <\s>
<s> she turns and goes quietly out barthwick <\s>
<s> the three barthwicks avoid each other's glances the curtain falls <\s>
<s> act ii scene i the jones's lodgings merthyr street at half past two o'clock <\s>
<s> the bare room with tattered oilcloth and damp distempered walls has an air of tidy wretchedness <\s>
<s> on the bed lies jones half dressed his coat is thrown across his feet and muddy boots are lying on the floor close by <\s>
<s> the door is opened and mrs <\s>
<s> jones comes in dressed in a pinched black jacket and old black sailor hat she carries a parcel wrapped up in the times <\s>
<s> she puts her parcel down unwraps an apron half a loaf two onions three potatoes and a tiny piece of bacon <\s>
<s> taking a teapot from the cupboard she rinses it shakes into it some powdered tea out of a screw of paper puts it on the hearth and sitting in a wooden chair quietly begins to cry <\s>
<s> soft and even unemphatic good morning sir <\s>
<s> about your husband he's not in work i hear <\s>
<s> no sir of course he's not in work just now <\s>
<s> then i suppose he's earning nothing <\s>
<s> no sir he's not earning anything just now sir <\s>
<s> and how many children have you <\s>
<s> three children but of course they don't eat very much sir <\s>
<s> a little silence barthwick <\s>
<s> and how old is the eldest <\s>
<s> nine years old sir <\s>
<s> do they go to school <\s>
<s> jones yes sir they all three go to school every day <\s>
<s> severely and what about their food when you're out at work <\s>
<s> well sir i have to give them their dinner to take with them <\s>
<s> of course i m not always able to give them anything sometimes i have to send them without but my husband is very good about the children when he's in work <\s>
<s> but when he's not in work of course he's a very difficult man <\s>
<s> he drinks i suppose <\s>
<s> of course i can't say he does n't drink because he does <\s>
<s> and i suppose he takes all your money <\s>
<s> no sir he's very good about my money except when he's not himself and then of course he treats me very badly <\s>
<s> now what is he your husband <\s>
<s> by profession sir of course he's a groom <\s>
<s> how came he to lose his place <\s>
<s> he lost his place a long time ago sir and he's never had a very long job since and now of course the motor cars are against him <\s>
<s> when were you married to him mrs <\s>
<s> eight years ago sir that was in mrs <\s>
<s> you said the eldest child was nine <\s>
<s> yes ma'am of course that was why he lost his place <\s>
<s> he did n't treat me rightly and of course his employer said he couldn't keep him because of the example <\s>
<s> you mean he ahem mrs <\s>
<s> yes sir and of course after he lost his place he married me <\s>
<s> you actually mean to say you you were barthwick <\s>
<s> hurriedly and where are you living now mrs <\s>
<s> we've not got a home sir <\s>
<s> of course we've been obliged to put away most of our things <\s>
<s> put your things away <\s>
<s> you mean to to er to pawn them <\s>
<s> yes sir to put them away <\s>
<s> we're living in merthyr street that is close by here sir at no <\s>
<s> we just have the one room <\s>
<s> and what do you pay a week <\s>
<s> we pay six shillings a week sir for a furnished room <\s>
<s> and i suppose you're behind in the rent <\s>
<s> yes sir we're a little behind in the rent <\s>
<s> but you're in good work aren't you <\s>
<s> well sir i have a day in stamford place thursdays <\s>
<s> and mondays and wednesdays and fridays i come here <\s>
<s> but to day of course is a half day because of yesterday's bank holiday <\s>
<s> i see four days a week and you get half a crown a day is that it <\s>
<s> yes sir and my dinner but sometimes it's only half a day and that's eighteen pence <\s>
<s> and when your husband earns anything he spends it in drink i suppose <\s>
<s> sometimes he does sir and sometimes he gives it to me for the children <\s>
<s> of course he would work if he could get it sir but it seems there are a great many people out of work <\s>
<s> we er won't go into that <\s>
<s> sympathetically and how about your work here <\s>
<s> do you find it hard <\s>
<s> no sir not very hard sir except of course when i don't get my sleep at night <\s>
<s> and you help do all the rooms <\s>
<s> and sometimes i suppose you go out for cook <\s>
<s> and you ve been out this morning <\s>
<s> yes sir of course i had to go to the greengrocer's <\s>

<s> you mean to to er to pawn them <\s>
<s> yes sir to put them away <\s>
<s> we're living in merthyr street that is close by here sir at no <\s>
<s> we just have the one room <\s>
<s> and what do you pay a week <\s>
<s> we pay six shillings a week sir for a furnished room <\s>
<s> and i suppose you're behind in the rent <\s>
<s> yes sir we're a little behind in the rent <\s>
<s> but you're in good work aren't you <\s>
<s> well sir i have a day in stamford place thursdays <\s>
<s> and mondays and wednesdays and fridays i come here <\s>
<s> but to day of course is a half day because of yesterday's bank holiday <\s>
<s> i see four days a week and you get half a crown a day is that it <\s>
<s> yes sir and my dinner but sometimes it's only half a day and that's eighteen pence <\s>
<s> and when your husband earns anything he spends it in drink i suppose <\s>
<s> sometimes he does sir and sometimes he gives it to me for the children <\s>
<s> of course he would work if he could get it sir but it seems there are a great many people out of work <\s>
<s> we er won't go into that <\s>
<s> sympathetically and how about your work here <\s>
<s> do you find it hard <\s>
<s> no sir not very hard sir except of course when i don't get my sleep at night <\s>
<s> and you help do all the rooms <\s>
<s> and sometimes i suppose you go out for cook <\s>
<s> and you ve been out this morning <\s>
<s> yes sir of course i had to go to the greengrocer's <\s>
<s> so your husband earns nothing <\s>
<s> and he's a bad character <\s>
<s> no sir i don't say that sir <\s>
<s> i think there's a great deal of good in him though he does treat me very bad sometimes <\s>
<s> and of course i don't like to leave him but i think i ought to because really i hardly know how to stay with him <\s>
<s> he often raises his hand to me <\s>
<s> not long ago he gave me a blow here touches her breast and i can feel it now <\s>
<s> so i think i ought to leave him don't you sir <\s>
<s> i can't help you there <\s>
<s> it's a very serious thing to leave your husband <\s>
<s> yes sir of course i m afraid of what he might do to me if i were to leave him he can be so very violent <\s>
<s> well that i can't pretend to say anything about <\s>
<s> it's the bad principle i'm speaking of mrs <\s>
<s> yes sir i know nobody can help me <\s>
<s> i know i must decide for myself and of course i know that he has a very hard life <\s>
<s> and he's fond of the children and its very hard for him to see them going without food <\s>
<s> hastily well er thank you i just wanted to hear about you <\s>
<s> i don't think i need detain you any longer mrs <\s>
<s> no sir thank you sir <\s>
<s> good morning sir good morning ma'am <\s>
<s> exchanging glances with his wife by the way mrs <\s>
<s> jones i think it is only fair to tell you a silver cigarette box er is missing <\s>
<s> looking from one face to the other i am very sorry sir <\s>
<s> yes you have not seen it i suppose <\s>
<s> realising that suspicion is upon her with an uneasy movement where was it sir if you please sir <\s>
<s> evasively where did marlow say <\s>
<s> er in this room yes in this room <\s>
<s> no sir i have n't seen it of course if i d seen it i should have noticed it <\s>
<s> giving hey a rapid glance you you are sure of that <\s>
<s> with a slow nodding of her head i have not seen it and of course i don't know where it is <\s>
<s> she turns and goes quietly out barthwick <\s>
<s> the three barthwicks avoid each other's glances the curtain falls <\s>
<s> act ii scene i the jones's lodgings merthyr street at half past two o'clock <\s>
<s> the bare room with tattered oilcloth and damp distempered walls has an air of tidy wretchedness <\s>
<s> on the bed lies jones half dressed his coat is thrown across his feet and muddy boots are lying on the floor close by <\s>
<s> the door is opened and mrs <\s>
<s> jones comes in dressed in a pinched black jacket and old black sailor hat she carries a parcel wrapped up in the times <\s>
<s> she puts her parcel down unwraps an apron half a loaf two onions three potatoes and a tiny piece of bacon <\s>
<s> taking a teapot from the cupboard she rinses it shakes into it some powdered tea out of a screw of paper puts it on the hearth and sitting in a wooden chair quietly begins to cry <\s>
<s> soft and even unemphatic good morning sir <\s>

<s> but when he's not in work of course he's a very difficult man <\s>
<s> he drinks i suppose <\s>
<s> of course i can't say he does n't drink because he does <\s>
<s> and i suppose he takes all your money <\s>
<s> no sir he's very good about my money except when he's not himself and then of course he treats me very badly <\s>
<s> now what is he your husband <\s>
<s> by profession sir of course he's a groom <\s>
<s> how came he to lose his place <\s>
<s> he lost his place a long time ago sir and he's never had a very long job since and now of course the motor cars are against him <\s>
<s> when were you married to him mrs <\s>
<s> eight years ago sir that was in mrs <\s>
<s> you said the eldest child was nine <\s>
<s> yes ma'am of course that was why he lost his place <\s>
<s> he did n't treat me rightly and of course his employer said he couldn't keep him because of the example <\s>
<s> you mean he ahem mrs <\s>
<s> yes sir and of course after he lost his place he married me <\s>
<s> you actually mean to say you you were barthwick <\s>
<s> hurriedly and where are you living now mrs <\s>
<s> we've not got a home sir <\s>
<s> of course we've been obliged to put away most of our things <\s>
<s> put your things away <\s>
<s> you mean to to er to pawn them <\s>
<s> yes sir to put them away <\s>
<s> we're living in merthyr street that is close by here sir at no <\s>
<s> we just have the one room <\s>
<s> and what do you pay a week <\s>
<s> we pay six shillings a week sir for a furnished room <\s>
<s> and i suppose you're behind in the rent <\s>
<s> yes sir we're a little behind in the rent <\s>
<s> but you're in good work aren't you <\s>
<s> well sir i have a day in stamford place thursdays <\s>
<s> and mondays and wednesdays and fridays i come here <\s>
<s> but to day of course is a half day because of yesterday's bank holiday <\s>
<s> i see four days a week and you get half a crown a day is that it <\s>
<s> yes sir and my dinner but sometimes it's only half a day and that's eighteen pence <\s>
<s> and when your husband earns anything he spends it in drink i suppose <\s>
<s> sometimes he does sir and sometimes he gives it to me for the children <\s>
<s> of course he would work if he could get it sir but it seems there are a great many people out of work <\s>
<s> we er won't go into that <\s>
<s> sympathetically and how about your work here <\s>
<s> do you find it hard <\s>
<s> no sir not very hard sir except of course when i don't get my sleep at night <\s>
<s> and you help do all the rooms <\s>
<s> and sometimes i suppose you go out for cook <\s>
<s> and you ve been out this morning <\s>
<s> yes sir of course i had to go to the greengrocer's <\s>
<s> so your husband earns nothing <\s>
<s> and he's a bad character <\s>
<s> no sir i don't say that sir <\s>
<s> i think there's a great deal of good in him though he does treat me very bad sometimes <\s>
<s> and of course i don't like to leave him but i think i ought to because really i hardly know how to stay with him <\s>
<s> he often raises his hand to me <\s>
<s> not long ago he gave me a blow here touches her breast and i can feel it now <\s>
<s> so i think i ought to leave him don't you sir <\s>
<s> i can't help you there <\s>
<s> it's a very serious thing to leave your husband <\s>
<s> yes sir of course i m afraid of what he might do to me if i were to leave him he can be so very violent <\s>
<s> well that i can't pretend to say anything about <\s>
<s> it's the bad principle i'm speaking of mrs <\s>
<s> yes sir i know nobody can help me <\s>
<s> i know i must decide for myself and of course i know that he has a very hard life <\s>
<s> and he's fond of the children and its very hard for him to see them going without food <\s>
<s> hastily well er thank you i just wanted to hear about you <\s>
<s> i don't think i need detain you any longer mrs <\s>
<s> no sir thank you sir <\s>
<s> good morning sir good morning ma'am <\s>
<s> exchanging glances with his wife by the way mrs <\s>
<s> jones i think it is only fair to tell you a silver cigarette box er is missing <\s>
<s> looking from one face to the other i am very sorry sir <\s>
<s> yes you have not seen it i suppose <\s>
<s> realising that suspicion is upon her with an uneasy movement where was it sir if you please sir <\s>
<s> evasively where did marlow say <\s>
<s> er in this room yes in this room <\s>
<s> no sir i have n't seen it of course if i d seen it i should have noticed it <\s>
<s> giving hey a rapid glance you you are sure of that <\s>
<s> with a slow nodding of her head i have not seen it and of course i don't know where it is <\s>
<s> she turns and goes quietly out barthwick <\s>

<s> act ii scene i the jones's lodgings merthyr street at half past two o'clock <\s>
<s> the bare room with tattered oilcloth and damp distempered walls has an air of tidy wretchedness <\s>
<s> on the bed lies jones half dressed his coat is thrown across his feet and muddy boots are lying on the floor close by <\s>
<s> the door is opened and mrs <\s>
<s> jones comes in dressed in a pinched black jacket and old black sailor hat she carries a parcel wrapped up in the times <\s>
<s> she puts her parcel down unwraps an apron half a loaf two onions three potatoes and a tiny piece of bacon <\s>
<s> taking a teapot from the cupboard she rinses it shakes into it some powdered tea out of a screw of paper puts it on the hearth and sitting in a wooden chair quietly begins to cry <\s>
<s> soft and even unemphatic good morning sir <\s>
<s> about your husband he's not in work i hear <\s>
<s> no sir of course he's not in work just now <\s>
<s> then i suppose he's earning nothing <\s>
<s> no sir he's not earning anything just now sir <\s>
<s> and how many children have you <\s>
<s> three children but of course they don't eat very much sir <\s>
<s> a little silence barthwick <\s>
<s> and how old is the eldest <\s>
<s> nine years old sir <\s>
<s> do they go to school <\s>
<s> jones yes sir they all three go to school every day <\s>
<s> severely and what about their food when you're out at work <\s>
<s> well sir i have to give them their dinner to take with them <\s>
<s> of course i m not always able to give them anything sometimes i have to send them without but my husband is very good about the children when he's in work <\s>
<s> but when he's not in work of course he's a very difficult man <\s>
<s> he drinks i suppose <\s>
<s> of course i can't say he does n't drink because he does <\s>
<s> and i suppose he takes all your money <\s>
<s> no sir he's very good about my money except when he's not himself and then of course he treats me very badly <\s>
<s> now what is he your husband <\s>
<s> by profession sir of course he's a groom <\s>
<s> how came he to lose his place <\s>
<s> he lost his place a long time ago sir and he's never had a very long job since and now of course the motor cars are against him <\s>
<s> when were you married to him mrs <\s>
<s> eight years ago sir that was in mrs <\s>
<s> you said the eldest child was nine <\s>
<s> yes ma'am of course that was why he lost his place <\s>
<s> he did n't treat me rightly and of course his employer said he couldn't keep him because of the example <\s>
<s> you mean he ahem mrs <\s>
<s> yes sir and of course after he lost his place he married me <\s>
<s> you actually mean to say you you were barthwick <\s>
<s> hurriedly and where are you living now mrs <\s>
<s> we've not got a home sir <\s>
<s> of course we've been obliged to put away most of our things <\s>
<s> put your things away <\s>
<s> you mean to to er to pawn them <\s>
<s> yes sir to put them away <\s>
<s> we're living in merthyr street that is close by here sir at no <\s>
<s> we just have the one room <\s>
<s> and what do you pay a week <\s>
<s> we pay six shillings a week sir for a furnished room <\s>
<s> and i suppose you're behind in the rent <\s>
<s> yes sir we're a little behind in the rent <\s>
<s> but you're in good work aren't you <\s>
<s> well sir i have a day in stamford place thursdays <\s>
<s> and mondays and wednesdays and fridays i come here <\s>
<s> but to day of course is a half day because of yesterday's bank holiday <\s>
<s> i see four days a week and you get half a crown a day is that it <\s>
<s> yes sir and my dinner but sometimes it's only half a day and that's eighteen pence <\s>
<s> and when your husband earns anything he spends it in drink i suppose <\s>
<s> sometimes he does sir and sometimes he gives it to me for the children <\s>
<s> of course he would work if he could get it sir but it seems there are a great many people out of work <\s>
<s> we er won't go into that <\s>
<s> sympathetically and how about your work here <\s>
<s> do you find it hard <\s>
<s> no sir not very hard sir except of course when i don't get my sleep at night <\s>
<s> and you help do all the rooms <\s>
<s> and sometimes i suppose you go out for cook <\s>
<s> and you ve been out this morning <\s>
<s> yes sir of course i had to go to the greengrocer's <\s>
<s> so your husband earns nothing <\s>
<s> and he's a bad character <\s>
<s> no sir i don't say that sir <\s>
<s> i think there's a great deal of good in him though he does treat me very bad sometimes <\s>
<s> and of course i don't like to leave him but i think i ought to because really i hardly know how to stay with him <\s>
<s> he often raises his hand to me <\s>
<s> not long ago he gave me a blow here touches her breast and i can feel it now <\s>
<s> so i think i ought to leave him don't you sir <\s>
<s> i can't help you there <\s>
<s> it's a very serious thing to leave your husband <\s>
<s> yes sir of course i m afraid of what he might do to me if i were to leave him he can be so very violent <\s>
<s> well that i can't pretend to say anything about <\s>
<s> it's the bad principle i'm speaking of mrs <\s>
<s> yes sir i know nobody can help me <\s>
<s> i know i must decide for myself and of course i know that he has a very hard life <\s>
<s> and he's fond of the children and its very hard for him to see them going without food <\s>
<s> hastily well er thank you i just wanted to hear about you <\s>
<s> i don't think i need detain you any longer mrs <\s>
<s> no sir thank you sir <\s>
<s> good morning sir good morning ma'am <\s>
<s> exchanging glances with his wife by the way mrs <\s>

<s> yes you have not seen it i suppose <\s>

<s> i can't help you there <\s>

<s> i know i must decide for myself and of course i know that he has a very hard life <\s>

<s> i don't think i need detain you any longer mrs <\s>

<s> act ii scene i the jones's lodgings merthyr street at half past two o'clock <\s>
<s> the bare room with tattered oilcloth and damp distempered walls has an air of tidy wretchedness <\s>
<s> on the bed lies jones half dressed his coat is thrown across his feet and muddy boots are lying on the floor close by <\s>
<s> the door is opened and mrs <\s>
<s> jones comes in dressed in a pinched black jacket and old black sailor hat she carries a parcel wrapped up in the times <\s>
<s> she puts her parcel down unwraps an apron half a loaf two onions three potatoes and a tiny piece of bacon <\s>
<s> taking a teapot from the cupboard she rinses it shakes into it some powdered tea out of a screw of paper puts it on the hearth and sitting in a wooden chair quietly begins to cry <\s>
<s> soft and even unemphatic good morning sir <\s>
<s> about your husband he's not in work i hear <\s>
<s> no sir of course he's not in work just now <\s>
<s> then i suppose he's earning nothing <\s>
<s> no sir he's not earning anything just now sir <\s>
<s> and how many children have you <\s>
<s> three children but of course they don't eat very much sir <\s>
<s> a little silence barthwick <\s>
<s> and how old is the eldest <\s>
<s> nine years old sir <\s>
<s> do they go to school <\s>
<s> jones yes sir they all three go to school every day <\s>
<s> severely and what about their food when you're out at work <\s>
<s> well sir i have to give them their dinner to take with them <\s>
<s> of course i m not always able to give them anything sometimes i have to send them without but my husband is very good about the children when he's in work <\s>
<s> but when he's not in work of course he's a very difficult man <\s>
<s> he drinks i suppose <\s>
<s> of course i can't say he does n't drink because he does <\s>
<s> and i suppose he takes all your money <\s>
<s> no sir he's very good about my money except when he's not himself and then of course he treats me very badly <\s>
<s> now what is he your husband <\s>
<s> by profession sir of course he's a groom <\s>
<s> how came he to lose his place <\s>
<s> he lost his place a long time ago sir and he's never had a very long job since and now of course the motor cars are against him <\s>
<s> when were you married to him mrs <\s>
<s> eight years ago sir that was in mrs <\s>
<s> you said the eldest child was nine <\s>
<s> yes ma'am of course that was why he lost his place <\s>
<s> he did n't treat me rightly and of course his employer said he couldn't keep him because of the example <\s>
<s> you mean he ahem mrs <\s>
<s> yes sir and of course after he lost his place he married me <\s>
<s> you actually mean to say you you were barthwick <\s>
<s> hurriedly and where are you living now mrs <\s>
<s> we've not got a home sir <\s>
<s> of course we've been obliged to put away most of our things <\s>
<s> put your things away <\s>
<s> you mean to to er to pawn them <\s>
<s> yes sir to put them away <\s>
<s> we're living in merthyr street that is close by here sir at no <\s>
<s> we just have the one room <\s>
<s> and what do you pay a week <\s>
<s> we pay six shillings a week sir for a furnished room <\s>
<s> and i suppose you're behind in the rent <\s>
<s> yes sir we're a little behind in the rent <\s>
<s> but you're in good work aren't you <\s>
<s> well sir i have a day in stamford place thursdays <\s>
<s> and mondays and wednesdays and fridays i come here <\s>
<s> but to day of course is a half day because of yesterday's bank holiday <\s>
<s> i see four days a week and you get half a crown a day is that it <\s>
<s> yes sir and my dinner but sometimes it's only half a day and that's eighteen pence <\s>
<s> and when your husband earns anything he spends it in drink i suppose <\s>
<s> sometimes he does sir and sometimes he gives it to me for the children <\s>
<s> of course he would work if he could get it sir but it seems there are a great many people out of work <\s>
<s> we er won't go into that <\s>
<s> sympathetically and how about your work here <\s>
<s> do you find it hard <\s>
<s> no sir not very hard sir except of course when i don't get my sleep at night <\s>
<s> and you help do all the rooms <\s>
<s> and sometimes i suppose you go out for cook <\s>
<s> and you ve been out this morning <\s>
<s> yes sir of course i had to go to the greengrocer's <\s>
<s> so your husband earns nothing <\s>
<s> and he's a bad character <\s>
<s> no sir i don't say that sir <\s>
<s> i think there's a great deal of good in him though he does treat me very bad sometimes <\s>
<s> and of course i don't like to leave him but i think i ought to because really i hardly know how to stay with him <\s>

<s> well sir i have a day in stamford place thursdays <\s>
<s> and mondays and wednesdays and fridays i come here <\s>
<s> but to day of course is a half day because of yesterday's bank holiday <\s>
<s> i see four days a week and you get half a crown a day is that it <\s>
<s> yes sir and my dinner but sometimes it's only half a day and that's eighteen pence <\s>
<s> and when your husband earns anything he spends it in drink i suppose <\s>
<s> sometimes he does sir and sometimes he gives it to me for the children <\s>
<s> of course he would work if he could get it sir but it seems there are a great many people out of work <\s>
<s> we er won't go into that <\s>
<s> sympathetically and how about your work here <\s>
<s> do you find it hard <\s>
<s> no sir not very hard sir except of course when i don't get my sleep at night <\s>
<s> and you help do all the rooms <\s>
<s> and sometimes i suppose you go out for cook <\s>
<s> and you ve been out this morning <\s>
<s> yes sir of course i had to go to the greengrocer's <\s>
<s> so your husband earns nothing <\s>
<s> and he's a bad character <\s>
<s> no sir i don't say that sir <\s>
<s> i think there's a great deal of good in him though he does treat me very bad sometimes <\s>
<s> and of course i don't like to leave him but i think i ought to because really i hardly know how to stay with him <\s>
<s> he often raises his hand to me <\s>
<s> not long ago he gave me a blow here touches her breast and i can feel it now <\s>
<s> so i think i ought to leave him don't you sir <\s>
<s> i can't help you there <\s>
<s> it's a very serious thing to leave your husband <\s>
<s> yes sir of course i m afraid of what he might do to me if i were to leave him he can be so very violent <\s>
<s> well that i can't pretend to say anything about <\s>
<s> it's the bad principle i'm speaking of mrs <\s>
<s> yes sir i know nobody can help me <\s>
<s> i know i must decide for myself and of course i know that he has a very hard life <\s>
<s> and he's fond of the children and its very hard for him to see them going without food <\s>
<s> hastily well er thank you i just wanted to hear about you <\s>
<s> i don't think i need detain you any longer mrs <\s>
<s> no sir thank you sir <\s>
<s> good morning sir good morning ma'am <\s>
<s> exchanging glances with his wife by the way mrs <\s>
<s> jones i think it is only fair to tell you a silver cigarette box er is missing <\s>
<s> looking from one face to the other i am very sorry sir <\s>
<s> yes you have not seen it i suppose <\s>
<s> realising that suspicion is upon her with an uneasy movement where was it sir if you please sir <\s>
<s> evasively where did marlow say <\s>
<s> er in this room yes in this room <\s>
<s> no sir i have n't seen it of course if i d seen it i should have noticed it <\s>
<s> giving hey a rapid glance you you are sure of that <\s>
<s> with a slow nodding of her head i have not seen it and of course i don't know where it is <\s>
<s> she turns and goes quietly out barthwick <\s>
<s> the three barthwicks avoid each other's glances the curtain falls <\s>
<s> act ii scene i the jones's lodgings merthyr street at half past two o'clock <\s>
<s> the bare room with tattered oilcloth and damp distempered walls has an air of tidy wretchedness <\s>
<s> on the bed lies jones half dressed his coat is thrown across his feet and muddy boots are lying on the floor close by <\s>
<s> the door is opened and mrs <\s>
<s> jones comes in dressed in a pinched black jacket and old black sailor hat she carries a parcel wrapped up in the times <\s>
<s> she puts her parcel down unwraps an apron half a loaf two onions three potatoes and a tiny piece of bacon <\s>
<s> taking a teapot from the cupboard she rinses it shakes into it some powdered tea out of a screw of paper puts it on the hearth and sitting in a wooden chair quietly begins to cry <\s>
<s> soft and even unemphatic good morning sir <\s>
<s> about your husband he's not in work i hear <\s>
<s> no sir of course he's not in work just now <\s>
<s> then i suppose he's earning nothing <\s>
<s> no sir he's not earning anything just now sir <\s>
<s> and how many children have you <\s>
<s> three children but of course they don't eat very much sir <\s>
<s> a little silence barthwick <\s>
<s> and how old is the eldest <\s>
<s> nine years old sir <\s>
<s> do they go to school <\s>
<s> jones yes sir they all three go to school every day <\s>
<s> severely and what about their food when you're out at work <\s>
<s> well sir i have to give them their dinner to take with them <\s>
<s> of course i m not always able to give them anything sometimes i have to send them without but my husband is very good about the children when he's in work <\s>
<s> but when he's not in work of course he's a very difficult man <\s>
<s> he drinks i suppose <\s>
<s> of course i can't say he does n't drink because he does <\s>
<s> and i suppose he takes all your money <\s>
<s> no sir he's very good about my money except when he's not himself and then of course he treats me very badly <\s>
<s> now what is he your husband <\s>
<s> by profession sir of course he's a groom <\s>
<s> how came he to lose his place <\s>
<s> he lost his place a long time ago sir and he's never had a very long job since and now of course the motor cars are against him <\s>
<s> when were you married to him mrs <\s>
<s> eight years ago sir that was in mrs <\s>
<s> you said the eldest child was nine <\s>
<s> yes ma'am of course that was why he lost his place <\s>
<s> he did n't treat me rightly and of course his employer said he couldn't keep him because of the example <\s>
<s> you mean he ahem mrs <\s>
<s> yes sir and of course after he lost his place he married me <\s>
<s> you actually mean to say you you were barthwick <\s>
<s> hurriedly and where are you living now mrs <\s>
<s> we've not got a home sir <\s>
<s> of course we've been obliged to put away most of our things <\s>
<s> put your things away <\s>
<s> you mean to to er to pawn them <\s>
<s> yes sir to put them away <\s>
<s> we're living in merthyr street that is close by here sir at no <\s>
<s> we just have the one room <\s>
<s> and what do you pay a week <\s>
<s> we pay six shillings a week sir for a furnished room <\s>
<s> and i suppose you're behind in the rent <\s>

<s> now what is he your husband <\s>
<s> by profession sir of course he's a groom <\s>
<s> how came he to lose his place <\s>
<s> he lost his place a long time ago sir and he's never had a very long job since and now of course the motor cars are against him <\s>
<s> when were you married to him mrs <\s>
<s> eight years ago sir that was in mrs <\s>
<s> you said the eldest child was nine <\s>
<s> yes ma'am of course that was why he lost his place <\s>
<s> he did n't treat me rightly and of course his employer said he couldn't keep him because of the example <\s>
<s> you mean he ahem mrs <\s>
<s> yes sir and of course after he lost his place he married me <\s>
<s> you actually mean to say you you were barthwick <\s>
<s> hurriedly and where are you living now mrs <\s>
<s> we've not got a home sir <\s>
<s> of course we've been obliged to put away most of our things <\s>
<s> put your things away <\s>
<s> you mean to to er to pawn them <\s>
<s> yes sir to put them away <\s>
<s> we're living in merthyr street that is close by here sir at no <\s>
<s> we just have the one room <\s>
<s> and what do you pay a week <\s>
<s> we pay six shillings a week sir for a furnished room <\s>
<s> and i suppose you're behind in the rent <\s>
<s> yes sir we're a little behind in the rent <\s>
<s> but you're in good work aren't you <\s>
<s> well sir i have a day in stamford place thursdays <\s>
<s> and mondays and wednesdays and fridays i come here <\s>
<s> but to day of course is a half day because of yesterday's bank holiday <\s>
<s> i see four days a week and you get half a crown a day is that it <\s>
<s> yes sir and my dinner but sometimes it's only half a day and that's eighteen pence <\s>
<s> and when your husband earns anything he spends it in drink i suppose <\s>
<s> sometimes he does sir and sometimes he gives it to me for the children <\s>
<s> of course he would work if he could get it sir but it seems there are a great many people out of work <\s>
<s> we er won't go into that <\s>
<s> sympathetically and how about your work here <\s>
<s> do you find it hard <\s>
<s> no sir not very hard sir except of course when i don't get my sleep at night <\s>
<s> and you help do all the rooms <\s>
<s> and sometimes i suppose you go out for cook <\s>
<s> and you ve been out this morning <\s>
<s> yes sir of course i had to go to the greengrocer's <\s>
<s> so your husband earns nothing <\s>
<s> and he's a bad character <\s>
<s> no sir i don't say that sir <\s>
<s> i think there's a great deal of good in him though he does treat me very bad sometimes <\s>
<s> and of course i don't like to leave him but i think i ought to because really i hardly know how to stay with him <\s>
<s> he often raises his hand to me <\s>
<s> not long ago he gave me a blow here touches her breast and i can feel it now <\s>
<s> so i think i ought to leave him don't you sir <\s>
<s> i can't help you there <\s>
<s> it's a very serious thing to leave your husband <\s>
<s> yes sir of course i m afraid of what he might do to me if i were to leave him he can be so very violent <\s>
<s> well that i can't pretend to say anything about <\s>
<s> it's the bad principle i'm speaking of mrs <\s>
<s> yes sir i know nobody can help me <\s>
<s> i know i must decide for myself and of course i know that he has a very hard life <\s>
<s> and he's fond of the children and its very hard for him to see them going without food <\s>
<s> hastily well er thank you i just wanted to hear about you <\s>
<s> i don't think i need detain you any longer mrs <\s>
<s> no sir thank you sir <\s>
<s> good morning sir good morning ma'am <\s>
<s> exchanging glances with his wife by the way mrs <\s>
<s> jones i think it is only fair to tell you a silver cigarette box er is missing <\s>
<s> looking from one face to the other i am very sorry sir <\s>
<s> yes you have not seen it i suppose <\s>
<s> realising that suspicion is upon her with an uneasy movement where was it sir if you please sir <\s>
<s> evasively where did marlow say <\s>
<s> er in this room yes in this room <\s>
<s> no sir i have n't seen it of course if i d seen it i should have noticed it <\s>
<s> giving hey a rapid glance you you are sure of that <\s>
<s> with a slow nodding of her head i have not seen it and of course i don't know where it is <\s>
<s> she turns and goes quietly out barthwick <\s>
<s> the three barthwicks avoid each other's glances the curtain falls <\s>

<s> jones comes in dressed in a pinched black jacket and old black sailor hat she carries a parcel wrapped up in the times <\s>
<s> she puts her parcel down unwraps an apron half a loaf two onions three potatoes and a tiny piece of bacon <\s>
<s> taking a teapot from the cupboard she rinses it shakes into it some powdered tea out of a screw of paper puts it on the hearth and sitting in a wooden chair quietly begins to cry <\s>
<s> soft and even unemphatic good morning sir <\s>
<s> about your husband he's not in work i hear <\s>
<s> no sir of course he's not in work just now <\s>
<s> then i suppose he's earning nothing <\s>
<s> no sir he's not earning anything just now sir <\s>
<s> and how many children have you <\s>
<s> three children but of course they don't eat very much sir <\s>
<s> a little silence barthwick <\s>
<s> and how old is the eldest <\s>
<s> nine years old sir <\s>
<s> do they go to school <\s>
<s> jones yes sir they all three go to school every day <\s>
<s> severely and what about their food when you're out at work <\s>
<s> well sir i have to give them their dinner to take with them <\s>
<s> of course i m not always able to give them anything sometimes i have to send them without but my husband is very good about the children when he's in work <\s>
<s> but when he's not in work of course he's a very difficult man <\s>
<s> he drinks i suppose <\s>
<s> of course i can't say he does n't drink because he does <\s>
<s> and i suppose he takes all your money <\s>
<s> no sir he's very good about my money except when he's not himself and then of course he treats me very badly <\s>
<s> now what is he your husband <\s>
<s> by profession sir of course he's a groom <\s>
<s> how came he to lose his place <\s>
<s> he lost his place a long time ago sir and he's never had a very long job since and now of course the motor cars are against him <\s>
<s> when were you married to him mrs <\s>
<s> eight years ago sir that was in mrs <\s>
<s> you said the eldest child was nine <\s>
<s> yes ma'am of course that was why he lost his place <\s>
<s> he did n't treat me rightly and of course his employer said he couldn't keep him because of the example <\s>
<s> you mean he ahem mrs <\s>
<s> yes sir and of course after he lost his place he married me <\s>
<s> you actually mean to say you you were barthwick <\s>
<s> hurriedly and where are you living now mrs <\s>
<s> we've not got a home sir <\s>
<s> of course we've been obliged to put away most of our things <\s>
<s> put your things away <\s>
<s> you mean to to er to pawn them <\s>
<s> yes sir to put them away <\s>
<s> we're living in merthyr street that is close by here sir at no <\s>
<s> we just have the one room <\s>
<s> and what do you pay a week <\s>
<s> we pay six shillings a week sir for a furnished room <\s>
<s> and i suppose you're behind in the rent <\s>
<s> yes sir we're a little behind in the rent <\s>
<s> but you're in good work aren't you <\s>
<s> well sir i have a day in stamford place thursdays <\s>
<s> and mondays and wednesdays and fridays i come here <\s>
<s> but to day of course is a half day because of yesterday's bank holiday <\s>
<s> i see four days a week and you get half a crown a day is that it <\s>
<s> yes sir and my dinner but sometimes it's only half a day and that's eighteen pence <\s>
<s> and when your husband earns anything he spends it in drink i suppose <\s>
<s> sometimes he does sir and sometimes he gives it to me for the children <\s>
<s> of course he would work if he could get it sir but it seems there are a great many people out of work <\s>
<s> we er won't go into that <\s>
<s> sympathetically and how about your work here <\s>
<s> do you find it hard <\s>
<s> no sir not very hard sir except of course when i don't get my sleep at night <\s>
<s> and you help do all the rooms <\s>
<s> and sometimes i suppose you go out for cook <\s>
<s> and you ve been out this morning <\s>
<s> yes sir of course i had to go to the greengrocer's <\s>
<s> so your husband earns nothing <\s>
<s> and he's a bad character <\s>
<s> no sir i don't say that sir <\s>
<s> i think there's a great deal of good in him though he does treat me very bad sometimes <\s>
<s> and of course i don't like to leave him but i think i ought to because really i hardly know how to stay with him <\s>
<s> he often raises his hand to me <\s>
<s> not long ago he gave me a blow here touches her breast and i can feel it now <\s>
<s> so i think i ought to leave him don't you sir <\s>
<s> i can't help you there <\s>
<s> it's a very serious thing to leave your husband <\s>
<s> yes sir of course i m afraid of what he might do to me if i were to leave him he can be so very violent <\s>
<s> well that i can't pretend to say anything about <\s>
<s> it's the bad principle i'm speaking of mrs <\s>
<s> yes sir i know nobody can help me <\s>
<s> i know i must decide for myself and of course i know that he has a very hard life <\s>
<s> and he's fond of the children and its very hard for him to see them going without food <\s>
<s> hastily well er thank you i just wanted to hear about you <\s>
<s> i don't think i need detain you any longer mrs <\s>
<s> no sir thank you sir <\s>
<s> good morning sir good morning ma'am <\s>
<s> exchanging glances with his wife by the way mrs <\s>
<s> jones i think it is only fair to tell you a silver cigarette box er is missing <\s>
<s> looking from one face to the other i am very sorry sir <\s>
<s> yes you have not seen it i suppose <\s>
<s> realising that suspicion is upon her with an uneasy movement where was it sir if you please sir <\s>
<s> evasively where did marlow say <\s>
<s> er in this room yes in this room <\s>
<s> no sir i have n't seen it of course if i d seen it i should have noticed it <\s>
<s> giving hey a rapid glance you you are sure of that <\s>
<s> with a slow nodding of her head i have not seen it and of course i don't know where it is <\s>
<s> she turns and goes quietly out barthwick <\s>
<s> the three barthwicks avoid each other's glances the curtain falls <\s>

<s> act ii scene i the jones's lodgings merthyr street at half past two o'clock <\s>
<s> the bare room with tattered oilcloth and damp distempered walls has an air of tidy wretchedness <\s>
<s> on the bed lies jones half dressed his coat is thrown across his feet and muddy boots are lying on the floor close by <\s>
<s> the door is opened and mrs <\s>
<s> jones comes in dressed in a pinched black jacket and old black sailor hat she carries a parcel wrapped up in the times <\s>
<s> she puts her parcel down unwraps an apron half a loaf two onions three potatoes and a tiny piece of bacon <\s>
<s> taking a teapot from the cupboard she rinses it shakes into it some powdered tea out of a screw of paper puts it on the hearth and sitting in a wooden chair quietly begins to cry <\s>
<s> soft and even unemphatic good morning sir <\s>
<s> about your husband he's not in work i hear <\s>
<s> no sir of course he's not in work just now <\s>
<s> then i suppose he's earning nothing <\s>
<s> no sir he's not earning anything just now sir <\s>
<s> and how many children have you <\s>
<s> three children but of course they don't eat very much sir <\s>
<s> a little silence barthwick <\s>
<s> and how old is the eldest <\s>
<s> nine years old sir <\s>
<s> do they go to school <\s>
<s> jones yes sir they all three go to school every day <\s>
<s> severely and what about their food when you're out at work <\s>
<s> well sir i have to give them their dinner to take with them <\s>
<s> of course i m not always able to give them anything sometimes i have to send them without but my husband is very good about the children when he's in work <\s>
<s> but when he's not in work of course he's a very difficult man <\s>
<s> he drinks i suppose <\s>
<s> of course i can't say he does n't drink because he does <\s>
<s> and i suppose he takes all your money <\s>
<s> no sir he's very good about my money except when he's not himself and then of course he treats me very badly <\s>
<s> now what is he your husband <\s>
<s> by profession sir of course he's a groom <\s>
<s> how came he to lose his place <\s>
<s> he lost his place a long time ago sir and he's never had a very long job since and now of course the motor cars are against him <\s>
<s> when were you married to him mrs <\s>
<s> eight years ago sir that was in mrs <\s>
<s> you said the eldest child was nine <\s>
<s> yes ma'am of course that was why he lost his place <\s>
<s> he did n't treat me rightly and of course his employer said he couldn't keep him because of the example <\s>
<s> you mean he ahem mrs <\s>
<s> yes sir and of course after he lost his place he married me <\s>
<s> you actually mean to say you you were barthwick <\s>
<s> hurriedly and where are you living now mrs <\s>
<s> we've not got a home sir <\s>
<s> of course we've been obliged to put away most of our things <\s>
<s> put your things away <\s>
<s> you mean to to er to pawn them <\s>
<s> yes sir to put them away <\s>
<s> we're living in merthyr street that is close by here sir at no <\s>
<s> we just have the one room <\s>
<s> and what do you pay a week <\s>
<s> we pay six shillings a week sir for a furnished room <\s>
<s> and i suppose you're behind in the rent <\s>
<s> yes sir we're a little behind in the rent <\s>
<s> but you're in good work aren't you <\s>
<s> well sir i have a day in stamford place thursdays <\s>
<s> and mondays and wednesdays and fridays i come here <\s>
<s> but to day of course is a half day because of yesterday's bank holiday <\s>
<s> i see four days a week and you get half a crown a day is that it <\s>
<s> yes sir and my dinner but sometimes it's only half a day and that's eighteen pence <\s>
<s> and when your husband earns anything he spends it in drink i suppose <\s>
<s> sometimes he does sir and sometimes he gives it to me for the children <\s>
<s> of course he would work if he could get it sir but it seems there are a great many people out of work <\s>
<s> we er won't go into that <\s>
<s> sympathetically and how about your work here <\s>
<s> do you find it hard <\s>
<s> no sir not very hard sir except of course when i don't get my sleep at night <\s>
<s> and you help do all the rooms <\s>
<s> and sometimes i suppose you go out for cook <\s>
<s> and you ve been out this morning <\s>
<s> yes sir of course i had to go to the greengrocer's <\s>
<s> so your husband earns nothing <\s>
<s> and he's a bad character <\s>
<s> no sir i don't say that sir <\s>
<s> i think there's a great deal of good in him though he does treat me very bad sometimes <\s>
<s> and of course i don't like to leave him but i think i ought to because really i hardly know how to stay with him <\s>
<s> he often raises his hand to me <\s>
<s> not long ago he gave me a blow here touches her breast and i can feel it now <\s>
<s> so i think i ought to leave him don't you sir <\s>
<s> i can't help you there <\s>
<s> it's a very serious thing to leave your husband <\s>
<s> yes sir of course i m afraid of what he might do to me if i were to leave him he can be so very violent <\s>
<s> well that i can't pretend to say anything about <\s>
<s> it's the bad principle i'm speaking of mrs <\s>

<s> of course he would work if he could get it sir but it seems there are a great many people out of work <\s>
<s> we er won't go into that <\s>
<s> sympathetically and how about your work here <\s>
<s> do you find it hard <\s>
<s> no sir not very hard sir except of course when i don't get my sleep at night <\s>
<s> and you help do all the rooms <\s>
<s> and sometimes i suppose you go out for cook <\s>
<s> and you ve been out this morning <\s>
<s> yes sir of course i had to go to the greengrocer's <\s>
<s> so your husband earns nothing <\s>
<s> and he's a bad character <\s>
<s> no sir i don't say that sir <\s>
<s> i think there's a great deal of good in him though he does treat me very bad sometimes <\s>
<s> and of course i don't like to leave him but i think i ought to because really i hardly know how to stay with him <\s>
<s> he often raises his hand to me <\s>
<s> not long ago he gave me a blow here touches her breast and i can feel it now <\s>
<s> so i think i ought to leave him don't you sir <\s>
<s> i can't help you there <\s>
<s> it's a very serious thing to leave your husband <\s>
<s> yes sir of course i m afraid of what he might do to me if i were to leave him he can be so very violent <\s>
<s> well that i can't pretend to say anything about <\s>
<s> it's the bad principle i'm speaking of mrs <\s>
<s> yes sir i know nobody can help me <\s>
<s> i know i must decide for myself and of course i know that he has a very hard life <\s>
<s> and he's fond of the children and its very hard for him to see them going without food <\s>
<s> hastily well er thank you i just wanted to hear about you <\s>
<s> i don't think i need detain you any longer mrs <\s>
<s> no sir thank you sir <\s>
<s> good morning sir good morning ma'am <\s>
<s> exchanging glances with his wife by the way mrs <\s>
<s> jones i think it is only fair to tell you a silver cigarette box er is missing <\s>
<s> looking from one face to the other i am very sorry sir <\s>
<s> yes you have not seen it i suppose <\s>
<s> realising that suspicion is upon her with an uneasy movement where was it sir if you please sir <\s>
<s> evasively where did marlow say <\s>
<s> er in this room yes in this room <\s>
<s> no sir i have n't seen it of course if i d seen it i should have noticed it <\s>
<s> giving hey a rapid glance you you are sure of that <\s>
<s> with a slow nodding of her head i have not seen it and of course i don't know where it is <\s>
<s> she turns and goes quietly out barthwick <\s>
<s> the three barthwicks avoid each other's glances the curtain falls <\s>
<s> act ii scene i the jones's lodgings merthyr street at half past two o'clock <\s>
<s> the bare room with tattered oilcloth and damp distempered walls has an air of tidy wretchedness <\s>
<s> on the bed lies jones half dressed his coat is thrown across his feet and muddy boots are lying on the floor close by <\s>
<s> the door is opened and mrs <\s>
<s> jones comes in dressed in a pinched black jacket and old black sailor hat she carries a parcel wrapped up in the times <\s>
<s> she puts her parcel down unwraps an apron half a loaf two onions three potatoes and a tiny piece of bacon <\s>
<s> taking a teapot from the cupboard she rinses it shakes into it some powdered tea out of a screw of paper puts it on the hearth and sitting in a wooden chair quietly begins to cry <\s>
<s> soft and even unemphatic good morning sir <\s>
<s> about your husband he's not in work i hear <\s>
<s> no sir of course he's not in work just now <\s>
<s> then i suppose he's earning nothing <\s>
<s> no sir he's not earning anything just now sir <\s>
<s> and how many children have you <\s>
<s> three children but of course they don't eat very much sir <\s>
<s> a little silence barthwick <\s>
<s> and how old is the eldest <\s>
<s> nine years old sir <\s>
<s> do they go to school <\s>
<s> jones yes sir they all three go to school every day <\s>
<s> severely and what about their food when you're out at work <\s>
<s> well sir i have to give them their dinner to take with them <\s>
<s> of course i m not always able to give them anything sometimes i have to send them without but my husband is very good about the children when he's in work <\s>
<s> but when he's not in work of course he's a very difficult man <\s>
<s> he drinks i suppose <\s>
<s> of course i can't say he does n't drink because he does <\s>
<s> and i suppose he takes all your money <\s>
<s> no sir he's very good about my money except when he's not himself and then of course he treats me very badly <\s>
<s> now what is he your husband <\s>
<s> by profession sir of course he's a groom <\s>
<s> how came he to lose his place <\s>
<s> he lost his place a long time ago sir and he's never had a very long job since and now of course the motor cars are against him <\s>
<s> when were you married to him mrs <\s>
<s> eight years ago sir that was in mrs <\s>
<s> you said the eldest child was nine <\s>
<s> yes ma'am of course that was why he lost his place <\s>
<s> he did n't treat me rightly and of course his employer said he couldn't keep him because of the example <\s>
<s> you mean he ahem mrs <\s>
<s> yes sir and of course after he lost his place he married me <\s>
<s> you actually mean to say you you were barthwick <\s>
<s> hurriedly and where are you living now mrs <\s>
<s> we've not got a home sir <\s>
<s> of course we've been obliged to put away most of our things <\s>
<s> put your things away <\s>
<s> you mean to to er to pawn them <\s>
<s> yes sir to put them away <\s>
<s> we're living in merthyr street that is close by here sir at no <\s>
<s> we just have the one room <\s>
<s> and what do you pay a week <\s>
<s> we pay six shillings a week sir for a furnished room <\s>
<s> and i suppose you're behind in the rent <\s>
<s> yes sir we're a little behind in the rent <\s>
<s> but you're in good work aren't you <\s>
<s> well sir i have a day in stamford place thursdays <\s>
<s> and mondays and wednesdays and fridays i come here <\s>
<s> but to day of course is a half day because of yesterday's bank holiday <\s>
<s> i see four days a week and you get half a crown a day is that it <\s>
<s> yes sir and my dinner but sometimes it's only half a day and that's eighteen pence <\s>
<s> and when your husband earns anything he spends it in drink i suppose <\s>
<s> sometimes he does sir and sometimes he gives it to me for the children <\s>
<s> of course he would work if he could get it sir but it seems there are a great many people out of work <\s>
<s> we er won't go into that <\s>
<s> sympathetically and how about your work here <\s>
<s> do you find it hard <\s>

<s> you mean he ahem mrs <\s>
<s> yes sir and of course after he lost his place he married me <\s>
<s> you actually mean to say you you were barthwick <\s>
<s> hurriedly and where are you living now mrs <\s>
<s> we've not got a home sir <\s>
<s> of course we've been obliged to put away most of our things <\s>
<s> put your things away <\s>
<s> you mean to to er to pawn them <\s>
<s> yes sir to put them away <\s>
<s> we're living in merthyr street that is close by here sir at no <\s>
<s> we just have the one room <\s>
<s> and what do you pay a week <\s>
<s> we pay six shillings a week sir for a furnished room <\s>
<s> and i suppose you're behind in the rent <\s>
<s> yes sir we're a little behind in the rent <\s>
<s> but you're in good work aren't you <\s>
<s> well sir i have a day in stamford place thursdays <\s>
<s> and mondays and wednesdays and fridays i come here <\s>
<s> but to day of course is a half day because of yesterday's bank holiday <\s>
<s> i see four days a week and you get half a crown a day is that it <\s>
<s> yes sir and my dinner but sometimes it's only half a day and that's eighteen pence <\s>
<s> and when your husband earns anything he spends it in drink i suppose <\s>
<s> sometimes he does sir and sometimes he gives it to me for the children <\s>
<s> of course he would work if he could get it sir but it seems there are a great many people out of work <\s>
<s> we er won't go into that <\s>
<s> sympathetically and how about your work here <\s>
<s> do you find it hard <\s>
<s> no sir not very hard sir except of course when i don't get my sleep at night <\s>
<s> and you help do all the rooms <\s>
<s> and sometimes i suppose you go out for cook <\s>
<s> and you ve been out this morning <\s>
<s> yes sir of course i had to go to the greengrocer's <\s>
<s> so your husband earns nothing <\s>
<s> and he's a bad character <\s>
<s> no sir i don't say that sir <\s>
<s> i think there's a great deal of good in him though he does treat me very bad sometimes <\s>
<s> and of course i don't like to leave him but i think i ought to because really i hardly know how to stay with him <\s>
<s> he often raises his hand to me <\s>
<s> not long ago he gave me a blow here touches her breast and i can feel it now <\s>
<s> so i think i ought to leave him don't you sir <\s>
<s> i can't help you there <\s>
<s> it's a very serious thing to leave your husband <\s>
<s> yes sir of course i m afraid of what he might do to me if i were to leave him he can be so very violent <\s>
<s> well that i can't pretend to say anything about <\s>
<s> it's the bad principle i'm speaking of mrs <\s>
<s> yes sir i know nobody can help me <\s>
<s> i know i must decide for myself and of course i know that he has a very hard life <\s>
<s> and he's fond of the children and its very hard for him to see them going without food <\s>
<s> hastily well er thank you i just wanted to hear about you <\s>
<s> i don't think i need detain you any longer mrs <\s>
<s> no sir thank you sir <\s>
<s> good morning sir good morning ma'am <\s>
<s> exchanging glances with his wife by the way mrs <\s>
<s> jones i think it is only fair to tell you a silver cigarette box er is missing <\s>
<s> looking from one face to the other i am very sorry sir <\s>
<s> yes you have not seen it i suppose <\s>
<s> realising that suspicion is upon her with an uneasy movement where was it sir if you please sir <\s>
<s> evasively where did marlow say <\s>
<s> er in this room yes in this room <\s>
<s> no sir i have n't seen it of course if i d seen it i should have noticed it <\s>
<s> giving hey a rapid glance you you are sure of that <\s>
<s> with a slow nodding of her head i have not seen it and of course i don't know where it is <\s>
<s> she turns and goes quietly out barthwick <\s>
<s> the three barthwicks avoid each other's glances the curtain falls <\s>
<s> act ii scene i the jones's lodgings merthyr street at half past two o'clock <\s>
<s> the bare room with tattered oilcloth and damp distempered walls has an air of tidy wretchedness <\s>

<s> the door is opened and mrs <\s>
<s> jones comes in dressed in a pinched black jacket and old black sailor hat she carries a parcel wrapped up in the times <\s>

<s> act ii scene i the jones's lodgings merthyr street at half past two o'clock <\s>
<s> the bare room with tattered oilcloth and damp distempered walls has an air of tidy wretchedness <\s>
<s> on the bed lies jones half dressed his coat is thrown across his feet and muddy boots are lying on the floor close by <\s>
<s> the door is opened and mrs <\s>
<s> jones comes in dressed in a pinched black jacket and old black sailor hat she carries a parcel wrapped up in the times <\s>
<s> she puts her parcel down unwraps an apron half a loaf two onions three potatoes and a tiny piece of bacon <\s>
<s> taking a teapot from the cupboard she rinses it shakes into it some powdered tea out of a screw of paper puts it on the hearth and sitting in a wooden chair quietly begins to cry <\s>
<s> soft and even unemphatic good morning sir <\s>
<s> about your husband he's not in work i hear <\s>
<s> no sir of course he's not in work just now <\s>
<s> then i suppose he's earning nothing <\s>
<s> no sir he's not earning anything just now sir <\s>
<s> and how many children have you <\s>
<s> three children but of course they don't eat very much sir <\s>
<s> a little silence barthwick <\s>
<s> and how old is the eldest <\s>
<s> nine years old sir <\s>
<s> do they go to school <\s>
<s> jones yes sir they all three go to school every day <\s>
<s> severely and what about their food when you're out at work <\s>
<s> well sir i have to give them their dinner to take with them <\s>
<s> of course i m not always able to give them anything sometimes i have to send them without but my husband is very good about the children when he's in work <\s>
<s> but when he's not in work of course he's a very difficult man <\s>
<s> he drinks i suppose <\s>
<s> of course i can't say he does n't drink because he does <\s>
<s> and i suppose he takes all your money <\s>
<s> no sir he's very good about my money except when he's not himself and then of course he treats me very badly <\s>
<s> now what is he your husband <\s>
<s> by profession sir of course he's a groom <\s>
<s> how came he to lose his place <\s>
<s> he lost his place a long time ago sir and he's never had a very long job since and now of course the motor cars are against him <\s>
<s> when were you married to him mrs <\s>
<s> eight years ago sir that was in mrs <\s>
<s> you said the eldest child was nine <\s>
<s> yes ma'am of course that was why he lost his place <\s>
<s> he did n't treat me rightly and of course his employer said he couldn't keep him because of the example <\s>
<s> you mean he ahem mrs <\s>
<s> yes sir and of course after he lost his place he married me <\s>
<s> you actually mean to say you you were barthwick <\s>
<s> hurriedly and where are you living now mrs <\s>
<s> we've not got a home sir <\s>
<s> of course we've been obliged to put away most of our things <\s>
<s> put your things away <\s>
<s> you mean to to er to pawn them <\s>
<s> yes sir to put them away <\s>
<s> we're living in merthyr street that is close by here sir at no <\s>
<s> we just have the one room <\s>
<s> and what do you pay a week <\s>
<s> we pay six shillings a week sir for a furnished room <\s>
<s> and i suppose you're behind in the rent <\s>
<s> yes sir we're a little behind in the rent <\s>
<s> but you're in good work aren't you <\s>
<s> well sir i have a day in stamford place thursdays <\s>
<s> and mondays and wednesdays and fridays i come here <\s>
<s> but to day of course is a half day because of yesterday's bank holiday <\s>
<s> i see four days a week and you get half a crown a day is that it <\s>
<s> yes sir and my dinner but sometimes it's only half a day and that's eighteen pence <\s>
<s> and when your husband earns anything he spends it in drink i suppose <\s>
<s> sometimes he does sir and sometimes he gives it to me for the children <\s>
<s> of course he would work if he could get it sir but it seems there are a great many people out of work <\s>
<s> we er won't go into that <\s>
<s> sympathetically and how about your work here <\s>
<s> do you find it hard <\s>
<s> no sir not very hard sir except of course when i don't get my sleep at night <\s>
<s> and you help do all the rooms <\s>
<s> and sometimes i suppose you go out for cook <\s>
<s> and you ve been out this morning <\s>
<s> yes sir of course i had to go to the greengrocer's <\s>
<s> so your husband earns nothing <\s>
<s> and he's a bad character <\s>
<s> no sir i don't say that sir <\s>
<s> i think there's a great deal of good in him though he does treat me very bad sometimes <\s>
<s> and of course i don't like to leave him but i think i ought to because really i hardly know how to stay with him <\s>
<s> he often raises his hand to me <\s>
<s> not long ago he gave me a blow here touches her breast and i can feel it now <\s>
<s> so i think i ought to leave him don't you sir <\s>
<s> i can't help you there <\s>
<s> it's a very serious thing to leave your husband <\s>
<s> yes sir of course i m afraid of what he might do to me if i were to leave him he can be so very violent <\s>
<s> well that i can't pretend to say anything about <\s>
<s> it's the bad principle i'm speaking of mrs <\s>
<s> yes sir i know nobody can help me <\s>
<s> i know i must decide for myself and of course i know that he has a very hard life <\s>
<s> and he's fond of the children and its very hard for him to see them going without food <\s>
<s> hastily well er thank you i just wanted to hear about you <\s>
<s> i don't think i need detain you any longer mrs <\s>
<s> no sir thank you sir <\s>
<s> good morning sir good morning ma'am <\s>
<s> exchanging glances with his wife by the way mrs <\s>
<s> jones i think it is only fair to tell you a silver cigarette box er is missing <\s>
<s> looking from one face to the other i am very sorry sir <\s>
<s> yes you have not seen it i suppose <\s>
